The Top 8 Decklists from the 2017 World Magic Cup
=================================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on December 2, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_EventCoverageStaff.jpg)
By Event Coverage Staff











Want to see what rose to the top of the 2017 World Magic Cup Then take a look at the Top 8 decklists!
